8. GM’s Choice

1-3 groups from other intelligent races (GM’s choice) (25% chance)

Durdeon Vislok and six members of the Sodality of the Fist: for stats, see AV-12.

### 6-71: Gladiators’ Preparation

* This lightly sanded hall serves as a practice facility and preparation hall for the gladiators of the Arena.
	* North wall: 10’-wide, 15’-tall opening into the Arena; a heavy portcullis (release is on the east wall) normally prevents exit. 
	* A steep stairway leads down to 6-72. 
	* Northeast and northwest walls: painted with enormous, art naïve images of smiling gladiators; above the images are the words ‘Honor’, ‘Comradeship’ and ‘Dignity’.

 * The gladiators enjoy a certain prestige among Arena attendees, but are technically bound in servitude to the Lord.
	 * Most have no intention of leaving; accustomed to the thrills and accolades of their position. 
	 * Their servile status is evident in the presence of guardsmen (6-74 and elsewhere).
* Bouts
	* Just before: selected gladiators meet here to oil themselves, swear sacred oaths to each other, and prepare their equipment.  6 guardsmen (from 6-74) will be present.
	* During: all gladiators not fighting are present here, pressed against the portcullis to witness the performances of their fellows.
	* Gladiators typically take part in one of the following types of bouts:
		* 1) 12 gladiators against each other
		* 2) 4-6 gladiators versus an outside team
		* 3) 3-4 gladiators versus some easy monsters

A list of the current gladiators living at the Arena (ranked from 1st to 15th)

(#1) Hector, 8th-level male Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL LN; AC 3; MV 120’; HD 8; HP 75; #AT 3/2; Dmg 6-13 (long sword +2), or 6-11 (spear +2). Abilities; STR 18/04, INT 8, WIS 10, 
DEX 16, CON 15, CHA 15. Possessions: orange-colored studded leather armor +2; long sword +2; spear +2; headband of the kallistos (see new magic items). 
* Personality: brave but dim; resents Tredgeris, poor judge of character; a talented fighter

### 6-72: Gladiators’ Hall (unmapped)

* This 30’ x 60’ x 15’ hall is reached via a steep staircase leading down from 6-71.
	* The floor is stone, covered with several inches of sand.
	* A continual light illuminates the area.
	* Against the east walls are the racks of gladiatorial weapons and equipment.
	* The walls are painted with over 300 life-like images of deceased gladiators, each in full gear and with his/her name listed beneath, some ancient and faded.
		* Desecration or ridicule of the images cause the entire gladiatorial troop to attack the blasphemer.
		* Two images of deceased gladiators are enchanted.
			* Lucius Magnus (halfway down the east wall) has enchanted eyes.
				* The Dapifer can see through them from his chambers (6-75).
				* The gladiators are aware, but most do not care.
			* Maria Bellatrix (just left of the staircase) is enchanted with luck.
				* Touching Maria’s whip bestows +1 to hit and immunity to extremes of heat and cold for three hours.
				* The gladiators and Dapifer know of this enchantment, but the Lord of the Arena does not.
* During a spectacle, the chamber is empty. If no spectacle is imminent, all of the gladiators (6-71) will be practicing here.

0-15 gladiators (stats at 6-71)

### 6-73: Cells of the Gladiators

* All of the gladiators except the top three live in this block of chambers, in one of the six cells with a door.
	* The walls are whitewashed stone, and lit by a continual light in the center of the entrance.
	* Cells are spartan, with simple cots, a few blankets, and a communal chest for a few personal items.
	* When the gladiators are present (8 hours per day), the doors are locked from the outside; when they are absent in 6-72 or in the Arena itself, the cells stand open.
* The door-less eastern niche features a latrine and a water basin.
* The gladiators’ winnings are kept in Hector’s chamber (6-78).

### 6-74: Guard Post

* The chamber is , and contains a trestle table, benches, and two large water barrels.
	* The walls are whitewashed stone, and brightly lit by continual light
* Six Arena guardsmen are posted here at all times, on a rotating basis (see 6-79).
	* When a spectacle is imminent or under way, the guardsmen are at 6-71.
	* Otherwise they kill time here, swapping lies and playing cards.  They pay little attention to the gladiators.

6 male Thorcin arena guardsmen, as 2nd-level fighters: SZ M; AL NE; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 2; HP 18, 17, 17, 16, 15, 15; #AT 1; Dmg 1-8 (long sword) or 1-6 (spear) or 1-4 (light crossbow). 
Possessions: scale mail; long swords; spears; light crossbow and 20 bolts; purse with 33 sp and 9 gp each. In addition to their mail byrnies, and simple helmets, they wear a light green surcoat emblazoned with a black image of a six-sided die.

### 6-75: Keeper of the Gladiators: Tredgeris the Dapifer

* A spacious chamber, home to the second-in-command of the Arena, a human named Tredgeris the Dapifer.
	* The chamber is door-less and illuminated by continual light.
	* A curtain divides the chamber in half.
		* North: public area with desk, a scroll cabinet, extra chairs, and a low table. 
			* Scroll Case: a dozen works of martial poetry (10-100 gp each), an ancient copy of the Lay of Marius Invictus by Lucius Cornelius (see 6-135 and books; worth only half the usual price); a scroll of protection from magic; 2 scrolls (legend lore; suggestion and mnemonic enhancer); the transcript of the testimony of a dying gladiator (provides accurate directions to the tomb of Marius Tricotor, 6-154, by way of 6-145 and 6-146.
			* Desk: a full psychological and physical assessment of all gladiators. Tredgeris has marked Yerk (6-77), Thomas (6-71) and Idris (6-71) as ‘beast-fodder’ and has starred Lara (6-76) as ‘the next Kallistos’.
		* South: private area, with comfortable feather bed, wardrobe, armor stand, a small table inset with a copper basin, and a locked ebony cabinet.
			* Copper basin: focusing on the water in the bowl for 2 rounds lets one scry from the vantage of the image of Lucius Magnus in 6-72.
			* South door: leads to a ledge overlooking the lesser chasm.
				* The bodies of slain gladiators are thrown into the pit.
				* Tredgeris knows of the passage west to 6-100, but hasn't explored it.
			* Locked Ebony Chest: 395 gp, 2,019 sp, 535 ancient silver pennies, and an olifant of command (struggling warriors) (new).
				* The chest itself is worth 400 gp.

Tredgeris the Dapifer
* A 48-year old male Archontean.
	* He began his career in Arden Vul as a slave of the Set Cult; the previous Dapifer purchased him from the Guild of Service and trained him as a gladiator.
	* Although never Kallistos, his intelligence meant that he was promoted to Dapifer six years ago.
		* Hector (6-78) resents this, and makes no secret of his hatred of Tredgeris.
		* Conversely, Tredgeris is supportive of Hector’s position as Kallistos, and is generally liked by the younger gladiators.
	* As Dapifer, it is Tredgeris’s responsibility to ensure that the Arena is staffed with a full complement of well-trained gladiators.
		* He is responsible for procuring new gladiators and overseeing training sessions (in 6-72).
	* Tredgeris is completely loyal to the Lord of the Arena.
* During and just before a spectacle, Tredgeris is found at the portcullis in 6-71.
* Otherwise he has a 50% chance to be here and 50% chance to be visiting 4-2 or 7-76.

Tredgeris, 7th-level male Archontean fighter (50% chance): SZ M; AL LN; AC 0; MV 220’; HD 7; HP 59; #AT 3/2; Dmg 5-11 (morning star +2). Abilities: STR 16, INT 15, WIS 15, DEX 15, 
CON 12, CHA 9. Possessions: chain mail +2; morning star +2; dagger; boots of speed; circlet of persuasion; and a purse with 204 gp.

### 6-76: Deuteros: Lara 

* The second and third ranked gladiators are called the Deuteroi (deuteros, sing.), and receive special treatment.  Lara, the number two gladiator, lives here.
	* She has a comfortable bed, a wardrobe, a small, unlocked chest, and the privilege of sleeping with her door unlocked.

Lara, 7th-level female Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL LN; AC 2; MV 120’; HD 7; HP 59; #AT 3/2; Dmg 5-10 (trident +2) or 3-6 (short sword +1). Abilities: STR 16, INT 15, WIS 11, DEX 17, CON 13, CHA 11. Possessions: studded leather +2; trident +2; short sword +1. She has a purse with 147 sp and 10 moonstone gems (50 gp each).
* Lara is a 35-year old woman, black-skinned, with an impressive scar on her right cheek.
* She is necessarily tough, and rarely swayed by sentiment.
* She has spent most of her life at the Arena and can think of nothing better than to be Kallistos.
* Her loyalty to the Lord (6-85) is abstract, but strong; she respects Tredgeris (6-75) and Hector (6-78), but has near contempt for Yerk (6-77).

### 6-77: Deuteros: Yerk

* Yerk, the number three gladiator and the other Deuteros, lives here. 
	* He has a comfortable bed, a wardrobe, a small, unlocked chest, and the privilege of sleeping with his door unlocked. 
 
Yerk, 7th-level male Thorcin fighter: SZ M; AL CN; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 7; HP 78; #AT 3/2; Dmg 6-7 (whip +2), or 6-13 (battle axe +2). Abilities; STR 18/23, INT 10, WIS 8, DEX 12, CON 
17, CHA 12. Possessions: whip +2; battle axe +2; studded leather armor +2.
* Yerk is a 30-year old human male who sports a mohawk and enjoys inscribing his own flesh with homemade tattoos.
* Yerk was a mercenary until captured a decade ago by the Guild of Service and sold to the Arena.
* He has risen to the rank of Deuteros mostly because he is utterly fearless and ruthless. 
* Indeed, all but Hector (6-78) suspect he is completely insane, while Lara (6-76) fears he may lose control in the near future.

### 6-78: Kallistos: Hector

* The first of the gladiators, or Kallistos, is Hector, who enjoys a life of relative ease in this spacious chamber.
	* His door remains unlocked, and he possesses a comfortable bed, a wardrobe, two locked chests, and a brandy rack.
		* Smaller locked chest: 560 sp, 113 ancient silver pennies, a pewter cup (25 sp).
		* Larger locked chest: 14 sacks with the winnings of the other gladiators, each containing 301-400 sp and 101-200 gp.

Hector, 8th-level male Archontean fighter: SZ M; AL LN; AC 3; MV 120’; HD 8; HP 75; #AT 3/2; Dmg 6-13 (long sword +2), or 6-11 (spear +2). Abilities; STR 18/04, INT 8, WIS 10, DEX 
16, CON 15, CHA 15. Possessions: orange-colored studded leather armor +2; long sword +2; spear +2; headband of the kallistos (see new magic items).
* Hector is male, Archontean, and 45 years old, with thinning brown hair and piercing grey eyes. He wears a silver mesh headband to indicate his rank.
* He has survived for 25 years in the Arena and can imagine no other life. He rose to the rank of Kallistos a decade ago, and expected to be made Dapifer.  When Tredgeris (6-75) was promoted above him, Hector was outraged and conceived a burning hatred for the new Dapifer. These feelings are starting to affect his competency as Kallistos, since he has interpreted Yerk’s psychotic behavior (6-77) as ‘good old-fashioned spirits’ rather than the dangerous insanity that it is.

### 6-79: Barracks of the Arena Guards 

* This chamber contains the bunkbeds and chests of the twenty guardsmen employed by the Lord of the Arena.
	* The walls are whitewashed, and the furniture is rough and simple.
	* The chest of each guardsman holds 5-100 sp and 5-30 gp.
	* During spectacles, only two guardsmen are present, otherwise, eight are present.
* The corridor to the south is blocked by a heavy portcullis
	* Raised by a lever on the south wall of 6-79.
* To the east the ceiling rises sharply to access the ballista post at 6-69.
	* A narrow staircase along the eastern wall allows the guardsmen to climb to that position.
* Along the north wall a spiral staircase leads down 20’ to an access tunnel.
	* This snakes under the Arena to emerge at another staircase leading up to 6-62.

2 or 8 male Thorcin arena guardsmen, as 2nd-level fighters: SZ M; AL NE; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 2; HP 19, 18, 17, 17, 16, 16, 15, 15; #AT 1; Dmg 1-8 (long sword) or 1-6 (spear) or 1-4 (light 
crossbow). Possessions: scale mail; long swords; spears; light crossbow and 20 bolts; purse with 33 sp and 9 gp each. In addition to their mail byrnies, and simple helmets, they wear a light green surcoat emblazoned with a black image of a six-sided die.

### 6-80: Commander of the Arena Guards

* Darko, commander of the guardsmen, inhabits this spartan chamber.
	* The walls are whitewashed and slightly dirty; a pair of smoky torches provides light.
	* Darko has a bed, desk, a pair of battered chairs, and a diverse collection of bottles both empty and full of noxious grain alcohol.
		* Desk drawer: a casket (200 ancient silver pennies, 399 gp).
		* Under the desk: a box containing 10 full and 20 empty bottles of brandy
			* One of the full bottles is fancy (250 gp), the others cheap (10-40 gp each).

* Darko is a drunkard, and spends most of his time in his room ‘working’ on duty rosters and tippling.
	* Although chronically impaired, he manages to fulfill his obligations and the Lord has not (yet) replaced him.

Darko, 5th-level male Thorcin fighter: SZ M; AL CE; AC 1; MV 90’; HD 5; HP 43; #AT 1; Dmg 3-10 (long sword +1) or 1-4 (light crossbow). Abilities: STR 16, INT 11, WIS 9, DEX 13, CON 15, CHA 9. Possessions: chain mail and shield +3; long sword +1; light crossbow, 20 quarrels.

### 6-81: Observation Window

* This sumptuously decorated chamber offers important visitors a comfortable location from which to view spectacles.
	* An 8' square window in the east wall overlooks the Arena.
	* The north and south walls are brightly painted with pastoral woodland scenes.
	* A plush orange carpet (50 gp) covers the floor.  3 leather chairs, a leather sofa, a low wooden table, and a teak humidor (50 gp) provide all the comforts one might need.

### 6-82: Solar 

* The Arena Lord’s salon is an elaborate, rococo riot of colors, fabrics, and objects.
	* The entire chamber is covered with thick plush orange carpet (of unknown substance). 
	* The walls are carved in elaborate mid-relief sculptures, all freshly painted in bright primary colors.
	* The sculptures show, clockwise from the east wall:
		* Writhing, intertwined figures in combat (tall skinny bipeds in uniforms, tall troll-like beings, and misshapen amphibian-oids; rudishva, varumani, and heqeti)
		* A huge flattened oval (matte black), with circular windows on it, surrounded by various unusual creatures.
		* Elaborate jungle and arboreal images, complete with unknown flora and fauna
		* A group of ten life-sized skinny bipeds (rudishva) wearing strange uniforms and gazing meaningfully toward the east. 
	* At the south end is a beautiful rosewood table inlaid with lapis, pearl, and silver
		* Four rosewood chairs surround it.
	* The rest of the chamber is stuffed with leather sofas, chairs, and ottomans, as well as with a rosewood sideboard, a rosewood scroll case, and a carved rosewood chest.
		* Eight pieces of bulky rosewood furniture (100-400 gp per piece).
		* Sideboard: heavy silver dining service (250 gp)
		* Scroll case:
			* 2 scrolls of protection from petrification; a scroll (tiny hut, tongues, water breathing); scroll (massmorph, wall of ice), scroll (animate dead, cloudkill); scroll (spirit-wrack, stone-to-flesh); scroll (monster summoning III, secret chest); scroll (levitate, locate object)
			* 16 scrolls describing in minute detail the spectacles staged in the Arena (these go back 500 years)
			* A scroll on unusual linen ‘parchment’ entitled the Time of Darkened Skies (books)
		* Chest: 6 heavy platinum goblets (100 gp each) in the chest; and 6 bottles of rudishva ‘aquavit’ (150 gp each).

### 6-83: Guest Room

* An orange plush carpet, overstuffed bed, and pair of leather chairs occupy this room.
	* The walls are painted a sea-green color.
* 20% chance the chamber is occupied by a guest (GM’s choice).

### 6-84: Lord’s Overlook

* The Lord of the Arena presides over spectacles from this brightly lit (continual light) overlook., 40’ above the floor of the Arena
	* Three onyx pillars support the aperture that gives forth to the Arena.
	* Four stone seats rest between the pillars, just at the edge of the floor.
	* Two gigantic eyes are painted on the northwest and southwest walls
		* An illusion, they appear to blink and regularly scan the Arena.
		* They are just cosmetic, but Arena regulars are convinced that they see all. 
* Haine, a rudishva military-grade security construct, stands just inside the west corridor
	* It is inert unless commanded into action by the Lord.
	* Haine once operated with all the same features as Relke (see 6-30), but has not been powered or charged for centuries.
		* His powered functions (flames, plasma beam, charged torso) no longer function.
		* If subdued Haine and brought to Kerbog Khan’s workshop, he might be restored to full functionality (see SL12-28).
* A miserable female goblin named Leila sleeps against the walls of this area.
	* She is the Lord’s personal servant, and is also responsible for ensuring that the sculptures in 6-82 are kept brightly painted.
	* Although she has been inside the Lord’s sanctum, both he and she prefer that she sleep elsewhere.

Lord of the Arena, only if a spectacle is underway (see stats at 6-85)

Leila, goblin servant: SZ S; AL LE; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 1-1; HP 3; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6.

Haine, partially-functioning military-grade rudishva security construct (see new monsters): SZ M; AL N; AC 3, MV 120’; HD 10; HP 50; #AT 2; Dmg 3-8/3-8 (fists); MR 50%. Special defenses: +2 weapons or better to hit; leap unerringly 30’; regenerate 2 HP/round. 

### 6-85: Lord of the Arena

* The insane, ancient Lord of the Arena counts this huge chamber as his inner sanctum.
	* The iris door that opens only to the Lord’s control bracelet.
	* The room is cool and dry, with light globes (tech) attached to the walls.
	* Each wall is freshly painted with trompe l’oeil techniques so each ‘wall’ appears as a corridor extending into the distance, the effect making the chamber seem larger than it is.
	* Most of the floor is covered with thick, plush orange carpet.
	* The corners of the chamber have been packed with cement and smoothed, so that no 90-degree angles are visible; though professionally done, it is obviously not original to the chamber.
* A 15’-diameter sunken, relaxation pool (4' deep) occupies the exact center of the chamber. 
* To the west stands the Lord’s massive, four-poster bed.
* To the north is a three-tiered display table, holding a variety of rare and exotic items.
	* Two fist-sized chunks of raw arcanum (see new magic items)
	* A 4”x10” holograph of the Lord standing with others of his race in front of a pile of amphibian corpses
	* A full set of Sortian eyes (new) mounted in a heavy silver necklace
	* The helm of Marius (new).
* To the southeast a 6’-tall egg-shaped object hangs from the ceiling.
	* One of only two rudishva portable medical units (tech) to remain operative (the other is in SL10a-32).
	* It has ensured the Lord’s longevity and continued health through judicious use over  roughly three millennia, though the process has effaced many of his memories.
* Northeast: three ‘troll’ chests, keyed to the Lord’s hand, and a pile of 3’-long cylinders.
	* Troll Chest 1: 40 lesser power supplies.
	* Stacked behind chest #1 are 10 greater power supplies (tech).
	* Troll Chest 2: laser rifle, laser pistol; 20 data crystals for a GnuCoder 5000 (see 5-97, mostly alien children’s stories), a pair of red plastic ducks; 3 frayed silk scarves; a set of keys to the Great Pillar (see 6-103); rudishva identity plaques (rust, brown, sky blue, pale green, pink, copper, bronze, and platinum).
	* Troll Chest 3: 18,473 cp; 7,599 sp; 5,321 gp; and 1,321 pp, plus a portable hole containing 20,000 ancient silver pennies, 5,000 ancient gold solidi, and 251 ancient octagonal platinum coins.
* Secret Door (west): in a trompe l’oeil image on the west wall, opens like a regular door.

Lord of the Arena
* The Lord appears as a skinny, 7’-tall biped with small horns protruding from the temples of his hairless head.
	* He wears a purple jumpsuit, white silk scarf, web-belt with holster, heavy varumani-skin boots, and several items of jewelry, including a torc of domination (new), his command bracelet (tech), and a beautiful topaz ring of levitation (new).
* Although he has lost memory of his name and former life, the Lord of the Arena was originally called Crellik-Var, and was the entertainment officer on the Beacon.
* He survived the heqeti plague through sheer genetic luck.
	* He and a few others (e.g. Psalor-Ki, 5-74) tried to maintain rudishva hegemony over the Halls.  When that failed, Crellik-Var migrated to this area, and began doing what he had always done – organize entertainment.
* Early in his career he recovered a number of rudishva objects from the halls, including the medical unit with which he prolonged his own life.
	* Extended use gradually effaced his identity, and now, despite being surrounded by familiar objects, Crellik-Var is truly and essentially the Lord of the Arena.
	* When his supply of power sources dries up, centuries from now, he will die.
* He lives only for the continuation of the spectacles and adherence to his own laws.
	* The embodiment of Lawful Neutral, he concerns himself not at all with the affairs of other parties, provided they adhere to his rules within his domain.
	* If encountered normally (at 6-58, 6-59 or 6-70) he is polite and terse.  He listens politely to all proposals but is only interested in those that aid in his agenda.
	* If visited unannounced in his sanctum, he is considerably less forgiving.
		* The Lord’s tactics are to summon the security construct (6-84), drink a potion of gaseous form, float out into the Arena, and rally his remaining servitors. He will use the ring of levitation and his laser pistol to good effect. 
	* If provided some great service (e.g. securing a particularly valuable monster for use in a spectacle), he may invite adventurers to spend 1d8 days as his guests in 6-83.
* If the Lord is slain, Tredgeris (6-75) vainly attempts to continue the Arena’s normal operations, but after 2-4 months the area collapses into anarchy.

The Lord of the Arena Crellik-Var, rudishva (see new monsters), with abilities of a 9th-level fighter; SZ L; AL LN; AC 4; MV 150’; HD 9; HP 64; #AT 6; Dmg 3-12/3-12/3-12/3-12/3-12/3-12.
* Implants: speed (AC 4; MV 150’; doubled attacks; haste for 1 turn/day), linguistics (comprehend and speak all languages), medical (regenerate 2 HP/round, 50% immunity to disease and poison), microprocessor (INT 18; +25% reaction rolls).
* Possessions
	* laser pistol
	* ring of levitation (new magic items)
	* torc of domination (see new magic items)
	* a command bracelet (see new technological items) that he uses to control both the environment globes in 6-70 and Haine, the military construct, in 6-84;
	* potion of gaseous form; potion of speed; a spare
	* full rudishva lesser power supply (see new technological items)
	* a silver rudishva identity plaque (see new technological items)
	* keys to the Great Pillar (6-103), appearing as 1’-long, 3”-diameter, grey plasteel rods with a notched, 1”-tall flange on each end.

##### 6-85a: Escape Tunnel 

* The secret door from 6-85 leads to a narrow, dark escape tunnel. 
	* From this tunnel, both secret doors are obvious to locate (3 in 4) and open.

### 6-86: Wranglers

* The Arena’s team of 20 expert monster-wranglers inhabits this simple, whitewashed chamber.
	* The west side is cluttered with 10 bunkbeds, a variety of chests and loose clothing, and scattered personal effects.
		* 149 gp, 457 sp total among the chests.
		* A dozen ½ oz doses of rastite lotus powder are hidden in various secret locations throughout their living quarters.
	* The east side of the room is a training area, and is kept scrupulously clean.
	* Several trophy heads, including a manticore, an owlbear, a dragonne, a pair of rhinoceros beetles, and a bulette, are mounted to the walls.
		* A potion of healing is concealed in the bulette’s maw.
	* Several racks holding all manner of whips, gaffs, goads, ankusas, long and short poles, ropes, and leather hoods stand against the walls. 
	* To the southeast a narrow staircase leads upwards to 6-69.
* If a spectacle is imminent or occurring, only 4 wranglers are present; otherwise 10.
	* Due to their frequent use of Rastite lotus powder (flora) in the pens (see 6-90 and 6-91), most of the wranglers are addicted to that drug.

8 goblin arena wranglers: SZ S; AL LE; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 1-1; HP 7, 6, 5(x3), 4, 4, 3; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6.

8 human arena wranglers: SZ M; AL N; AC 8; MV 120’; HD 1-1; HP 7, 7, 6, 6, 5, 5, 4, 4; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6 (spear). Possessions: leather armor; spear.

4 lesser varumani (see new monsters) arena wranglers: SZ L; AL LE; AC 4; MV 90’; HD 8; HP 61, 59, 58, 57; #AT 3 or 1; Dmg 3-6/3-6/4-10 or 7-22 (club, 3-18+4). Special defenses: 33% 
resistant to mind-affecting magic; immune to cold and poison; save as 8th-level fighters or 8th-level magic users, whichever is better; regenerate 3 HP/rd; infravision. Possessions: clubs.

### 6-87: Monster Preparation Area
 
* This 25’-tall, sandy-floored chamber is where the wranglers prepare monsters for spectacles in the Arena.
	* Two 12’-tall arches lead into the Arena; heavy portcullises normally close them off.
	* Further sets of portcullises impede entrance to and from the pens. 

### 6-88: Kitchen

* This smoke-blackened room swirls with odors both pleasant and not.
	* A fireplace and chimney occupy the east wall.
	* To the north are several huge cabinets in which the cook has stacked various preserved meats, vegetables, and mushrooms.
	* The preparation table is to the south.
	* By the entrance door is a basin and enormous water barrel.
	* The cook, an ancient beastman runaway, sleeps under the preparation table.

Ancient beastman cook, as a trooper (see new monsters): SZ S; AL LE; AC 9; MV 90’; HD 1+1; HP 4; #AT 1; Dmg 1-3 (cleaver).

### 6-89: Monster Pens, Small

* Five pens for smaller monsters occupy this 25’-tall, bi-level space.
	* New monsters are brought along 6-58, through the door to the pens, then simply push the monster from the eastern walkway into the appropriate 10’x10’x15’ pen.
		* Climbing or flying monsters are contained in their pens by special covers that lean against the east wall.  Similar covers rest against the lower grates when the pens house monsters with breath weapons.
		* Each pen has a stone trough and some rancid straw. The monsters are fed irregularly, and are snarly and dangerous. 
	* To bring the monsters forth:
		* Smudge pots laced with Rastite lotus powder (flora) are tossed into the pens.  The drugged smoke rendering monsters briefly pliant and non-aggressive.
		* The iron grates are raised via a pulley system attached to the ceiling; wranglers stand on the eastern, upper walkway and pull.
		* Other wranglers swarm into the pen behind heavy, tower-style shields and secure the creatures via goads, snares, nets, and so forth. 
* The southeast corner holds a rack with the ropes, goads, nets, hoods, snares, and other devices necessary for wrangling. 
* At the north end of the chamber are stairs linking upper and lower levels.

* The Arena will replace creature within 3d6 days.
	* Contracts to procure live monsters from the Nether Reaches may be arranged with Tredgeris the Dapifer (6-75).
* At present, the pens hold:

A: 6 giant bombardier beetles: SZ M; AL N; AC 4; MV 90’; HD 2+2; HP 17, 16, 14, 13, 13, 12; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: acid cloud (50% chance per round).

B: 3 hell hounds: SZ M; AL LE; AC 4; MV 120’; HD 5; HP 35, 32, 31; #AT 1; Dmg 1-10. Special attacks: breathe fire; surprise on 1-4 in 6. Special defenses: surprised only on 1 in 6. Special: 50% to spot hidden or invisible.

C: A smoke mephit and a steam mephit. 
* 1 smoke mephit: SZ M; AL CE; AC 4; MV 120’, 240’ flying (Class B); HD 3; HP 19; #AT 2; Dmg 1-2/1-2. Special attacks: breath weapon; flame damage on death. Special: invisibility (1/day); dancing lights (1/day); gate 1-2 mephits (20% chance).
* 1 steam mephit: SZ M; AL NE; AC 7; MV 120’, 240’ flying (Class B); HD 3+3; HP 21; #AT 2; Dmg 1-4/1-4. Special attacks: breath weapon once every other round; boiling rainstorm 1/day; contaminate water 1/hour. Special defenses: steaming skin; gate another mephit 1/hour (30% chance).

D: Empty

E: 5 ghouls: SZ M; AL CE; AC 6; MV 90’; HD 2; HP 13, 12, 11, 11, 10; #AT 3; Dmg 1-3/1-3/1-6. Special attacks: paralysis. Special defenses: immune to sleep and charm.

### 6-90: Storage

* A whitewashed storage chamber.
	* A dozen smudge pots
	* A locked chest
		* 30 doses of Rastite lotus powder,6 of Gethite lotus powder (flora)
	* Two dozen bales of straw
		* Tucked behind the hay is a greater salt lamp of protection (new).
	* Numerous spare parts for the wranglers
	* Eight sets of gladiator equipment
	* 12 small or medium corpses hanging from hooks in the ceiling (monster chow)
* There is a 50% chance that any item of adventuring gear can be found in this chamber.

### 6-91: Monster Pens, Large

* The larger pens work the same way as the smaller ones (6-89).
	* Pens are 20’x20’20’.
	* Beasts (groggy with rastite smoke) are maneuvered out out of the pens through the iron portcullises on the south side (20’ below the northern walkway).
		* The portcullises raise via a set of pulleys set into the 30’-tall ceiling.
	* Removable lids to seal the tops of pens rest against the north wall, along with iron-and-wooden baffles to be pushed against the portcullises when a pen houses a monster with a breath weapon.
* Numerous hooks holding snares, prods, and so forth are scattered throughout the chamber. 

* Larger monsters take a 6d6 days to replace.

Current inhabitants of the pens include:

A: 1-2 manticores: SZ L; AL LE; AC 4; MV 120’, 180’ flying (Class E); HD 6+3; HP 47, 40; #AT 3; Damage 1-3/1-3/1-8. Special attacks: four sets of 6 tail spikes (1-6 HP/spike).

B: 1 fire lizard: SZ L; AL N; AC 3, MV 90’; HD 10; HP 67; #AT 3; Dmg 1-8/1-8/2-16. Special attacks: breath weapon (2-12 HP). Special defenses: immune to fire.

C: 1 chimera: SZ L; AL CE; AC 6/5/2, MV 90’, 180’ flying (Class E); HD 9; HP 61; #AT 6; Dmg 1-3/1-3/1-4/1-4/2-8/3-12. Special attacks: breath weapon (3-24 HP).

D: 2 owlbears: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 5+2; HP 39, 33; #AT 3; Dmg 1-6/1-6/2-12. Special attacks: hug.

E: 2 giant scorpions: SZ M; AL N; AC 3; MV 150’; HD 5+5; HP 39, 35; #AT 3; Dmg 1-10/1-10/1-4. Special attacks: poison.

## Level 6: 92 - 105

### 6-92: Hall of Stone Heads

* The 30’-tall hall is in bad shape, with cracked and buckled floor tiles and numerous mini-collapses from the ceiling and walls.
	* Dates to the heqeti period, with the usual grey, oily, pebbled stonework.
	* The hall is dominated by a row of impressive, 5’-diameter stone face pillars.
		* Including the special guardian head (6-94) and the head isolated by a cave-in (6-104), four heads survive in this hall. 
		* Each rises 15’ to the ceiling and is carved with grotesque amphibian features (bulbous eyes, slit noses and lolling tongues). The mouth of each head/face is open, revealing a 2’ oval compartment. 
			* If a flask of ‘sweat’ from 6-93 is placed in a mouth, the tongue of that head licks the nearest person (within 5’).  They will be able to recognize and open all secret doors and passages on Level 6 (including 6-95a), and be afflicted with an effect from the following table.

D10 Effect

1 Sweat uncontrollably for 7 days, -3 CHA, -1 to hit rolls
2 Temporary gills for 7 days, allowing subject to breathe underwater
3 Eyes grow disproportionately large for 3 days, -1 CHA but true seeing
4 Legs grow in power while arms atrophy for 3 days: MV increased by 30’, STR -1
5 Webbing between fingers and toes, 50% better swimming but -1 CHA
6 Comprehend amphibian tongues, for 7 days
7 Cursed (if Good), Blessed for 3 days if CE.  Nothing for other alignments
8 Sensitive to light for 7 days (-2 to all rolls), but gains infravision
9 Locate body of fresh water; knows route to pool-sized bodies of water or larger w/in 200’
10 Mark of Kauket: all 9 of the above, 1-3 of the effects are permanent.

* Remove curse will remove any of the temporary negative effects, but the Mark of Kauket can only be removed via alter reality, miricle, limited wish or wish, or through the special favor of a good-aligned deity via the completion of a significant quest.

### 6-93: Sweating Antechamber

* The chamber is sheathed in the same ancient, oily, pebbled stone as the rest of this area.
	* It ‘sweats’ an odorless, viscous, clear liquid, slowly but steadily.
		* No special properties, except it is used to manipulate the Stone Heads in 6-92.
	* Sweat pools along the cracked flagstones of the floor. 

### 6-94: Guardian Head

* An archway leads to a 15’-tall extension of the hall of stone heads (6-92), where still one more head stares towards the west.
	* The head is humanoid with fish-eyes, feather-gills, and an open mouth.
	* Adding ‘sweat’ from 6-93 causes the same effects as the other stone heads (6-92).
	* The Lord of the Arena (6-85) has added further enchantments to this head.
		* If anyone other than the Lord enters this chamber, guardian starts to shout loud imprecations (Heqeti): ‘Get away, you ever-cursed Monkey-Boys! This area is not for you!’ This goes on for a turn, with a 50% chance to alert the Lord (if present in areas 6-82 to 6-85). 

### 6-95: Hall of Four Pillars

* This extension of the Hall of Stone Heads is 30' tall and features four greasy, smoothed-granite pillars (numbered from south to north, radiating magic) holding up the roof.
	* Touching a pillar adjusts features of the large rudishva face.
		* Pillar 1: reset (eyes and mouth closed, nostrils flared) 
		* Pillar 2: the mouth opens wide
		* Pillar 3: the nostrils close up
		* Pillar 4: the eyes open wide
	* Attached to the north wall is a 5' tall, high-relief sculpture of rudishva face (also radiating magic) that is a secret door (difficult).
		* Default state: eyes and mouth closed, nostrils flared.
		* If the pillars are touched in order 3-4-2 (nostrils, eyes, mouth), the mouth gapes to reveal a 5' circular tunnel into 6-95a.
		* Any other sequence causes the Guardian Head at 6-94 to begin yelling curses.
	* The door to 6-57 is kept locked, and is difficult to pick (-10%). 
	* Secret Door (east, to 6-85a): difficult (1 in 8) to detect from 6-95, opens by sliding a stone panel to one side.

##### 6-95a: Rudishva Chamber

* Beyond the rudishva face is a gleaming chamber sheathed in white marble tiles.
	* All corners are rounded, with no 90-degree angles present.
	* In the center, three orange plasteel benches surround a 5’-diameter sunken spot in the floor. Whatever once filled the basin is long gone.
* The westernmost section (10’x20’) is a elevator leading up through a shaft in the ceiling 1,050’ to SL2-3.
	* On the south wall next to the elevator is an inlay of lapis, showing a 6”-diameter orb surrounded by three 2”-diameter orbs (the rudishva homeworld and its moons). 
		* Touching it summons the elevator.
	* The elevator is present 50% of the time, otherwise a rough patch of unfinished granite marks its footprint.
		* When it arrives, those under it must save vs breath or be crushed to death.
	* The elevator is a slab of polished blue granite, with a similar lapis inlay incised in the center. The inlay shows a 1’ orb with three 4” orbs around it. 
		* Touching the inlay activates the elevator.  Cumulative 1% per use that the elevator ceases to function.
* To the east sits a node in the rudishva teleportation network.
	* A 5’-diameter circle of silvery material inset into the floor, with a 10”x10” square of the same material affixed to the wall, marked with a rune.
	* T4: access to 5-92 (Translocation Hub)
* On the south wall, a 5’-diameter circle has been cut out of the regular white marble.
	* Beyond the circle is the back side (teeth) of the stone face in 6-95.
	* A 12”-long, ½”-wide slot is set in the lip of the circle. Inserting a rod causes the mouth to open, granting access to 6-95.  While it stays inserted, the face stays open; if removed, it closes after 1 turn.

### 6-96: The Arena Lord’s Stash

* This unadorned chamber has the pebbled, oily walls of ancient heqeti construction.
* A standard Archontean-era door (locked) has been added.
	* On the floor just inside the door are warding chain of glyphs (fire, 7 glyphs - see new spells).
* Piled haphazardly within are large, bulky items salvaged by the Arena Lord over the centuries. 
	* A working mobile stone cutter (see new technological items)
	* Irreparably broken Nutri-Vore 2000 and Gnu-Coder 5000
	* 6 depleted rudishva greater power supplies
	* A pair of 6’-tall, 4’-diameter clay urns incised with bipedal salamanders (ancient heqeti burial urns, 200 gp, 150 lb each)
	* Two 4’-diameter kegs of Archontean brandy (1/4 and 1/3 full, 150 and 200 gp)
	* A brass, ivory, and colored glass orrery, 5’ tall (250 gp)
	* 6 petrified roc eggs (25 gp each)
	* A bizarre Archontean mechanical ‘bank’ (575 gp).
		* 4' tall and depicting the impalement of a criminal.
		* To operate, deposit an ancient silver penny or gold solidus into the executioner’s pouch; the criminal is automatically lowered onto the impalement stake while his mouth opens in a silent scream).
		* The mechanical bank holds 23 ancient silver pennies and 5 ancient gold solidi.
* Due to the cave-ins in the surrounding areas (6-97), most of stored items won't fit through the narrow tunnel leading to 6-92.
	* 4-6 hours of digging with hand tools, or 4-6 turns with the mobile stone cutter, will widen the tunnel sufficiently (cumulative 15% chance per hour of causing a cave-in, 4d10 dmg and burying the diggers).

### 6-97: Corridor Fragment

* This section of the old main corridor is still in relatively good shape, despite the cave-ins that surround it.
	* At the western edge of the fragment is the mostly-buried body of an adventurer.
		* Digging her out takes 2-4 turns, with a 1-in-6 chance / turn to cause further collapse (3d6).
		* Corpse: the Kauketiad (books), an ancient rudishva description of the ziggurat of Kauket (areas 10-32 to 10-35); a bag of holding (150 cubic feet capacity) with  407 ancient silver pennies, 119 ancient gold solidi, short sword +2, and a varumani skull with a thick wax candle melted onto it (15 sp).
	* The narrow (3’x5’) tunnel to the west is hard to spot amid all the rubble (3 in 8).

### 6-98: Rubble-Filled Tunnel and Closet

* The narrow access tunnel connecting 6-105 and 6-97 is filled with rubble and impassable.
	* 12-18 hours of careful digging could clear the tunnel.
	* Each hour has a 1 in 6 chance of a cave-in (3d6, lose 1d3 hour of digging progress).
	* A small closet (7’ tall, 4’ square) still exists to the north of the rubble-filled tunnel.
		* Amid some rotted litter is a copper rudishva identity plaque.

### 6-99a: Stasis Bridge (North) and Fiery Dancer

* A 3’-radius sphere of white marble is embedded in the granite at the end of this corridor; An identical sphere waits 30’ away on the south side of the chasm.
	* The two spheres are the bases of a rudishva stasis bridge.
	* Rectangular indentations 6” x 2” in size are visible in the marble spheres.
		* Placing a silver identity plaque in either indentation causes a 1’-wide band of buzzing silver energy to appear, linking the two spheres.
		* Though narrow, the stasis bridge is perfectly safe and remains for 2 turns after the identity plaque is removed.
* Fifteen feet north of the white marble sphere a rudishva fiery force shield blocks the entire corridor.
	* As with the shield at 5-90a, the flame is broken only by an 8’-tall, 4’-wide oval in which a holographic figure stands on one leg.
		* The figure has two legs and six arms, holding a drum, pot of fire, lotus, and dagger; the other two hands hold nothing.
	* If any living being approaches within 5’, the six-armed figure starts to dance, beginning slowly but swiftly increasing its tempo.
		* After 3 rounds, the whirling figure begins to call hurl blobs of fire from the force wall, unerringly striking for d6 fire (may ignite combustibles). 
	* The force wall can only be destroyed by disintegration.
	* Presenting an orange, silver, or yellow identity plaque after the figure has begun to dance causes it to dematerialize and passage through the oval opening.
		* After a turn, the dancer rematerializes.

### 6-99b: Stasis Bridge (South)

* For appearance and operation of the stasis bridge, see 6-99a.
* The iris door to the east opens to an orange or silver rudishva identity plaque.
	* Once opened, the door reveals a rudishva tunnel leading to 6-100.

### 6-100: Hangar with Hover Sled

* Both doors to this hangar are rudishva iris doors that open to orange or silver rudishva identity plaques.
* The opening to the chasm is concealed by a heavy curtain of vines.
	* Noisy activity near these vines is 75% likely to attract the huge spiders that lair in the chokepoint leading to 6-101.
* The hangar holds a hover sled salvaged by the Arena Lord after the Archontean collapse.
	* The chamber is sheathed in white marblewith no 90-degree angles.
	* The Lord has not used the sled in over 500 years, but it is still in good working order.
		* A laser rifle and two lesser power supplies are stored in the sled.

### 6-101: Lesser Chasm

* This chasm is connected to the Great Chasm by a very narrow passage currently jammed with cave vines and creepers.
	* A nest of huge spiders has made its home near this chokepoint.
	* They take particular interest in any attempting to access 6-100 via the passage on the west wall of the chasm.

8 huge spiders: SZ M; AL N; AC 6; MV 180’; HD 2+2; HP 17, 16, 15, 14, 14, 13, 12, 11; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6. Special attacks: surprise 1-5; poison (+1 to saves); can leap up to 30’.

### 6-102: A Pair of Huge – and Occupied - Seats 

* These chairs, carved from oily soapstone emitting a faint tinge of ancient evil, are identical to those at 6-63 (10’ wide, 15’ tall, and 5’ deep, with seats 5’ off the floor). 
	* Two giant rudishva skeletons are seated (which keeps the nosy away from 6-103). 
	* The Arena Lord (6-85) has not sent a cleanup detail this way in some time.  Several corpses – including two goblins impaled with femur bones – are scattered around.
		* Among the corpses: 35 gp, 77 sp, a purse with 10 pieces of jade (100 gp each), 2 potions of healing, scroll (false trap, haste, and fear).
* Secret Door (north): opens when an orange or silver rudishva identity plaque is held before a 2” circle of glowing red light.

2 semi-intelligent giant rudishva skeletons: SZ L; AL NE; AC 2; MV 90’; HD 8+8; HP 68, 54; #AT 1 or 2; Dmg 3-18 (weapon) or 2-8/2-8 (bone throwing); MR 50%. Special attacks: bone 
throwing; sonic blast. Special defenses: +1 or better weapons to hit; half damage from sharp or edged weapons; half damage from fire; immune to sleep, charm, cold, poison, and paralysis.

### 6-103: Great Pillar

* The Great Pillar, which begins on Level 5 (5-138), continues downward here.
	* General description of the Great Pillar (see 5-138). 
		* No bridge to the central shaft exists at this level.
		* The pod of chasm cephalopods (5-138) can be attracted to 6-103 as well.
	* From this location it can be used to reach 5-138, 7-37 and 9-30.
	* The three iris doors require a special key to unlock (-40% to pick, wizard locked (12th level)).
		* The troll thegn (7-30) and the Arena Lord (6-85) each possess a key.
		* The keys are 1’-long, 3”-diameter, grey plasteel rods with a notched, 1”-tall flange on each end.

### 6-104: Lost Shrine to Rimmaq-Isfet

* At the eastern end of the Hall of Stone Heads is a newly restored shrine to Rimmaq-Isfet.
	* Since cave-ins, it had been lost for over a millennium, and only recently rediscovered by a heqeti exploration party.
	* The worked areas have cracked, buckled granite floor tiles, and pebbled, oily walls.
* To the east, one of the stone heads (see 6-92) marks the edge of a major cave-in.
	* It can be manipulated in the same way as the other stone heads. 
* The tunnel leading west and south to the Chasm is new construction, shining with slime.
	* A pair twisted vine ropes is stapled to the entrance of this corridor; it runs close to the Chasm face and leads to 6-107.  The heqeti use the ropes to move between 6-106 and 6-104. Using the ropes requires a successful roll under STR on 2d6.
* The southeastern extension is freshly carved, used as the campground of the heqeti group.
	* Strange woven bags of dried fish and mushrooms, and a large bucket of slime.
* The shrine proper lies to the west, in front of the new tunnel leading out to the Chasm.
	* A 15’-tall, 3’-wide oval pool of murky, viscous brown sludge.
		* At the bottom is a fast-rotting leather sack (235 sp, 456 gp, and 122 pp), bronze and rust rudishva identity plaques, and a gold Sortian eye.
	* Four 4' tall slim columns of polished basalt placed around the pool, one on each side, set obliquely (not perpendicular to the floor).
	* When the proper summoning rites have been performed, a worm of Qok (new) appears in the pool, eager to devour whatever sacrifices are forthcoming. 
* A party of heqeti is present here to guard the recovered shrine.
	* A builder leads a chosen, a weaver, and three hoppers.
	* They have captured three adventurers, and bound them to the basalt columns as sacrifices to Rimmaq-Isfet.
	* Two rounds into any combat, the worm of Qok arrives in the pool, seeking to swallow whatever prey is making the most noise nearby. 
* This hall is a destination for the heqeti teleporter located at area 10-8.

1 heqeti builder (see new monsters), 6th/6th-level fighter/cleric of Rimmaq-Isfet: SZ M; AL CE; AC 1; MV 90’, 120’ swimming; HD 6; HP 46; #AT 1; Dmg 4-9 (short sword +2 of wounding). Constant abilities: infravision. Special attacks: +1 to damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and water/ice.
* Possessions: heqeti mail armor (-2 to AC); short sword +2 of wounding, amulet of natural armor +2 (see new magic items).
* Spells: bless, command, cure light wounds, light, fear; chant, hold person (x2), silence 15’ radius, speak with animals; dispel magic, curse.

1 heqeti weaver (see new monsters), as a 5th-level magic user: SZ M; AL CE; AC 5; MV 120’, 90’ swimming; HD 5; HP 16; #AT 1; Dmg 1-3 (darts). Constant abilities: infravision. Special attacks: +1 to damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and water/ice.
* Possessions: brooch of shielding (56 HP left); 6 poisoned darts.
* Memorized spells: jump, magic missile, protection from good, sleep; invisibility, mirror image; lightning bolt. 
* Spell book: dancing lights, detect magic, enlarge, jump, magic missile, protection from good, read magic, shield, sleep; darkness 15’ radius, invisibility, knock, mirror image, ray of enfeeblement, strength; blink, dispel magic, gust of wind, lightning bolt, slow.

1 heqeti chosen (see new monsters), as a 6th-level fighter: SZ M; AL CE; AC 5; MV 60’, 150’ swimming; HD 6; HP 39; #AT 2; Dmg 2-7 (spear), 1-6 (bite). Special attacks: hop; acid tongue (1-6 acid damage); +1 damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold and water/ice.

3 heqeti hoppers (see new monsters), as 4th-level fighters: SZ M; AL CE; AC 5; MV 60’, 150’ swimming; HD 4; HP 28, 26, 24; #AT 2; Dmg 2-7 (spear), 1-6 (bite). Special attacks: hop; +1 to damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and water/ice.

1 worm of Qok (see new monsters): SZ L; AL CE; AC 3; MV 60’; HD 12; HP 86; #AT 1; Dmg 2-24; MR 50%. Special attacks: swallow.

Odd of Freyr’s Landing, 4th-level male Wiskin ranger: SZ M; AL CG; AC 10; MV 120’; HD 4; HP 21 (max 40); #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 16, INT 13, WIS 14, DEX 11, CON 16, CHA 8. Possessions: none.

Helgi of Westholm, 3rd-level male Wiskin cleric of Bragi: SZ M; AL CG; AC 9; MV 120’; HD 3; HP 18; #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 16, INT 10, WIS 17, DEX 15, CON 10, CHA 15. Possessions: none. Spells: bless, create water, cure light wounds (x2); slow poison, speak with animals.

Kerrie Flaxseed, 5th-level female halfling thief: SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 90’; HD 5; HP 24; #AT 1; Dmg by weapon. Abilities: STR 11, INT 14, WIS 15, DEX 18, CON 13, CHA 15. Thief skills: PP 
65%, OL 62%, F/RT 50%, MS 60%, HS 56%, HN 25%, CW 75%, RL 20%. Possessions: none.

### 6-105: Wet Chamber

* The heqeti exploration party that refurbished 6-106 placed several alarm and defense mechanisms in this chamber.
	* The walls are newly coated with a white, paint-like slime that is eating away the rudishva-era murals underneath.
		* Those murals are now unintelligible on all but the north wall, which shows a trio of rudishva pointing narrow sticks/wands at a mass of amphibian-oids.
	* The northern part of this chamber is wet with a gray-green, nutrient slime, out of which grow 3 shriekers.
		* The shriekers are likely to draw the heqeti hoppers from 6-106.
	* Clinging to the ceiling is a large gray ooze.
* The narrow tunnel leading east is filled with rubble (see 6-98).
* Secret Door (west): newly constructed and easy to locate (1 in 4).
	* Opens to brute force (stuck door or total 30 STR from up to 2 characters).

3 shriekers: SZ M; AL N; AC 7; MV 10’; HD 3; HP 19, 14, 13; #AT 0; Dmg nil. Special attacks: noise.

1 gray ooze: SZ L; AL N; AC 8; MV 10’; HD 3+3; HP 23; #AT 1; Dmg 2-16. Special attacks: corrode metal. Special defenses: impervious to spells; immune to heat and cold. 

## Level 6: 106 - 136

### 6-106: Heqeti Transport Chamber

* The first chamber on Level 6 that the resurgent heqeti refurbished, providing access to several important heqeti locations deeper in the Halls.
	* The walls are coated with slime to slowly render them pebbled and greasy/oily.
	* The stairs lead down in a tight spiral to the Nether Reaches (8-25)
	* The tunnel to the east is newly carved and still wet with slime.
* The niches to the north contain heqeti teleport wells.
	* Each well is a 7’-diameter circle of stone rising 3’ above the floor.
		* The righthand well is operative, containing nothing but inky blackness (anything entering emerges at 10-24).
	* The lefthand well is inoperative, just a 10’-deep well with a carven image of an gape-mouthed (4' hole) amphibian head at the bottom.
		* Normally, dropping a tear of Kauket (new) into the mouth would reactivate it; but the enchantments are broken.
* Secret Door (north): opens by sliding a stone panel upwards into a slot in the wall.
	* Beyond, a narrow corridor and 5’ flight of stairs lead up to 6-51.
* Secret Door (east, to 6-105): easy to locate (1 in 4), opened by brute force (stuck door or 30 STR from up to 2 characters).
* If the hoppers on guard hear the shriekers in 6-105, they will investigate in 2 rounds.

4 heqeti hoppers (see new monsters), as 4th-level fighters: SZ M; AL CE; AC 5; MV 60’, 150’ swimming; HD 4; HP 28, 26, 24, 22; #AT 2; Dmg 2-7 (spear), 1-6 (bite). Special attacks: hop; +1 to damage due to STR; toxic skin (paralysis for 1-2 rounds). Special defenses: psionic resistance; immune to sleep, charm, hold, and water/ice.

### 6-107: Pukel-mander

* Another of the heqeti pukel-manders (new) squats in this chamber.
	* A pile of bricks (one side carved to resemble natural stone) rests on either side of the pukel-mander.
		* A wall that shielded the pukel-mander from the Great Chasm was recently  destroyed (natural stone carved side was concealment).
	* Two ropes made of vines are stapled to the southeast wall, leading to the new tunnel to 6-104.
* Secret Door (north): opens when a button in a ½”-diameter hole in the floor is pressed.  It is freshly oiled and maintained.

### 6-108: Great Chasm

* One of the iconic features of the Halls, this massive fissure extends through most of the dungeon levels and provides a sure, if difficult, means of vertical navigation of the Halls.
	* The fissure is generally shaped like a triangular prism, its apex ~50’ above Level 2.
	* The prism extends downward 1,600’ through the Halls until leveling out at the floor of the chasm (9-1).
* At this level the chasm is noisy with life and activity. 
	* The warmth given off by the Floating Garden (6-4) and the moisture from the waterfalls ensures abundant plant and insect life.
	* Creepers, vines, lichen mats, and so forth line the walls.
	* To the southeast, a nest of huge spiders has taken up residence in the bottleneck leading to the lesser chasm (6-101).

* Secret Door (to 6-19a, locked, -20% to pick): difficult to spot (1 in 8) from the chasm.

* Random encounters use the following table; 1-in-6 per 3 turns.

### 6-109: Stone Corridor 

* This stone corridor leads from the Great Pillar to the residential pod of the Beacon.
	* As per 6-103, the rudishva iris door leading to the Pillar is unusual, as it is wizard locked (12th level) and requires a key to open.
	* The corridor is dusty and absent signs of recent traffic.
	* Sounds of crunching metal are audible from the west.

### 6-110: Slagged Corridor with Xorn

* Here , where the corridor changes from stone to plasteel, a tremendous battle took place in antiquity.
* The plasteel walls and floor have buckled and melted, with burn and scorch marks around a 30’-deep pit of slagged plasteel.
	* In the center of the pit are 2 xorn, happily munching on the metallic bounty. 

2 xorn: SZ M; AL N; AC -2; MV 90’; HD 7+7; HP 55, 49; #AT 4; Dmg 1-3/1-3/1-3/6-24. Special attacks: surprise on 1-5. Special defenses: immune to fire and cold; half damage from electricity; travel through stone.

### 6-111: Plasteel Corridor

* The corridor is plasteel, metallic and white, and conveys sound easily.
* A rudishva iris door leads to the residential pod.
	* Opens to a brown, sky blue, pale green, orange, pink, silver, or yellow ID plaque.
	* The wall around the door is grey plassteel, not quite as smooth (micro-pitted).
		* Added after the crash, not part of the original ship.
* A 5’-diameter hole has been slagged through the plasteel of the south wall, east of the door to 6-112.
	* A rope hangs through the hole into area 6-112, held in place by an ‘x’ made of two 6’ pieces of wood nailed together.
	* GM Note: the Bad Neighbors (6-113) made the hole with their laser rifle and used the rope to shimmy down into 6-112.
### 6-112: Cavern with Residential Pod and Access to SL4-28

* One of the residential pods from the Beacon dominates this large cavern.
	* In the crash, it was driven (half-out of phase) through the rock materializing and leaving a burn hole extends upward 475’ to SL4-28. 
	* The floor of the cavern has been levelled, but its walls remain rough rock.
	* The cavern is warm due to pod's energy emission.  Numerous vines, creepers, lichens, and molds grow here.
		* Creepers grow up and enshroud the pod, and can be climbed to the roof.
		* A pack of vicious subterranean lizards resides here.  They hunt using the vines and creepers for height and surprise.
	* The grey plasteel residential pod is 40’ tall, resting on several sets of sturdy tripod legs.
		* The pod's south end was corroded away in antiquity (by the sumuksu , still in 6-121), leaving an 8’x15’ hole 25’ up from the cavern floor. 

7 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 45, 42, 39, 37, 36, 33, 32; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 6-112a: Heqeti Statue and Tunnel to 9-39

* Squatting on a ledge overlooking the cavern is a heqeti statue.
	* Lacking the potency of the ancient pukel-manders, it is an 8’ tall statue carved from soapstone of a salamander-thing with powerful legs and a salamander head.
	* Its over-sized eyes are disks of quartz (50 gp each).
	* Behind the statue, a tunnel wends its way downward to 9-39. 

### 6-113: Residential Pod of the Beacon, Upper Level

* The pod can be accessed either through the door to 6-111 or the corroded hole leading to 6-112; both entrances lead to the upper level of the residential pod.
	* All structural surfaces are white plasteel, with interior walls featuring decorative swooshes and swirls in a variety of primary colors.
	* The hallway is dirty, scattered with trash, lizard skins, and numerous bones (mostly from small animals).
	* A 3’-wide, sickening-brown smear of partly melted plasteel runs down the center of the hallway and up to each door.
		* GM Note: produced by the sumuksu, still residing in 6-121).
	* The nuclear reactor for this pod is still active (6-123) and lighting is still operational throughout the residential pod.
		* LED strips run along the corridor ceilings.  30' segments will be motion-activated weight >25 lb on the deck.
* The oval central chamber of the pod contains two null-grav holes in the floor leading to the lower level.
	* One steps into the hole, gives a shove, and levitates downward to emerge at 6-118. 

* The Bad Neighbors, a party of evil NPC adventurers, lurk in the corridor just north of the central chamber.
	* Members include: Klibo, Haldor, Idris One-Eye, Uriel Bean, Wotar the Puny, and Qid of Qon
	* They acquired two laser rifles, using them to cut the hole at 6-111 and to drive off the lizards of 6-112.
	* They used a Reduce (reverse of Enlarge) to squeeze between the cavern wall of 6-112 and the bulkhead of the residential pod.
	* If they hear intruders, they prepare an ambush with spells and laser fire.
	* Their base camp is located at 6-129.

### 6-114: Crew Quarters (x8)

* These eight chambers are roughly egg-shaped, with a lack of 90-degree angles.
	* Doors are 6’-diameter iris doors, all jammed ‘open’ since antiquity.
	* Entering a chamber illuminates it with a peaceful yellow glow from a hanging fixture.
	* A 2’-wide smear of brown corrosion runs through each open door and into the center of each room; a product of the sumuksu (6-121).
* Each chamber contains a pair of wall-mounted bunk beds mounted over a desk, two wardrobes, and a vacuum sink; these are built into the wall.  Two orange hard-plastic chairs affixed to the floor (25% chance the adhesive has deteriorated, 25 gp each).
	* All movable furnishings were stripped long time ago, and there is a jumble of trash (desiccated vines, broken bits of plasteel, fragments of parchment, small bones, and bits of leather gear).
		* Each turn of searching has 25% chance of finding something from the chart (max two finds per chamber, results can't repeat in different rooms).

D20 Item Notes
* 1 Flute made from a polished femur 
* 2 Silk purse with 35 gp
* 3 Cracked leather purse with 22 ancient silver pennies
* 4 A marble finger broken off of a long-lost statue; a silver ring (25 sp) is jammed onto it
* 5 A pair of illuminated parchment folios with the Reception of Light canticle from the Litany of Light
	* For the canticle, see 2-3; for the Litany of Light. Folios are worth 20 gp.
* 6 A troll thegn’s Passport (av items)
* 7 A straw doll (3” tall) of a goblin dressed in fancy robes with a needle for a sword.
	* The doll belonged to Gribble (3-105B), the brother of King Weskenim (SL4-22). Weskenim will pay 45 gp for the nostalgia it brings.
* 8 An empty rudishva lesser power supply, with “I need more of these!” written on it (Archontean).
* 9 A rust, copper, bronze or brown rudishva identity plaque (25% chance for each)
* 10 A piece of ebony carved to resemble a heqeti hopper (25 gp).
* 11 A rudishva data crystal (tech), marked with glyph for ‘home’.
	* Used in a GnuCoder 5000 (5-97), it displays cheesy home movies of a rudishva crewman and his friends visiting strange alien worlds.
* 12 Two arrows +2
* 13 Copper torc with black boar engraved on it (25 sp)
	* The boar refers to the cult of Set (see Level 4)
* 14 Deck of playing cards with blue snake on reverse
* 15 A desiccated body (d8), stripped of equipment.
	* 1-4: human, 5: goblin, 6: varumani, 7: dwarf, 8: rudishva
* 16 Coil of silk rope, 50’
* 17 A soft-gel package of ancient rudishva brandy (50% spoiled, otherwise 250 gp)
* 18 A necklace of human teeth strung on a piece of rawhide
* 19 A heqeti stone-tipped spear; the shaft is carved with amphibian warriors (5 gp)
* 20 A fragment of plasteel etched with writing (Glyphik): “The slime has breached the hull. We are doomed. The kaliyani are to blame. I will retreat to my quarters and die honorably.”
	* Refers to the sumuksu (6-121) that compromised the living quarters. Also contains a hint as to the culpability of the kaliyani in the downfall of the rudishva.

### 6-115: Empty Officers’ Quarters (x2)

* These two rooms are larger versions of the crew quarters (6-114), clad in white plasteel, with wall-mounted bed and a desk, closet, and orange plastic chair all affixed to the floor.
	* The doors to both chambers have been eaten open by some corrosive agent, leaving a jagged, 4’-diameter entrance and tell-tale brown smear of corrosive leading into each chamber (the sumuksu in 6-121).
	* Littered with trash (searching is 50% likely per turn to turn up one of the items from the table at 6-114).

### 6-116: Officer’s Quarters, Occupied

* Identical to 6-115 (complete with corroded ‘door’), except it has become the lair of an enormous boa constrictor.
	* The boa perches on the wall-mounted bed.  It has a good chance of surprising any but the most cautious of explorers.
* The floor of the chamber is littered with even more litter, much of it bones.
	* Among the bones are scattered 35 sp, 47 gp, and 14 pp.

1 giant constrictor snake: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 90’; HD 6+1; HP 39; #AT 2; Dmg 1-4/2-8. Special attacks: constriction.

### 6-117: Officer’s Quarters, Intact

* The iris door to this chamber is intact and opens to a sky blue, silver, or yellow identity plaque.
	* No smear of brown corrosion enters this chamber.
* The basic features of the chamber are identical to those in 6-115.
	* The desiccated corpse of Mol-Prev, the Beacon’s Morale Officer, hangs by a noose attached to the light fixture.
		* He committed suicide when the sumuksu (6-121) breached the hull and the heqeti assault commenced.
	* Desk:
		* Two holo-cubes (personal pictures of Mol-Prev in a variety of formal (full-dress uniform) and informal (carousing with mates) poses) (500 gp each)
		* One bracelet from a pair of communication bracelets; the other is in SL6-55)
		* A GnuCoder 3000 Data Recorder
		* Drawer 1: three fully-charged lesser power supplies and two blank data crystals for the GnuCoder.
		* Drawer 2: a plastic box with twelve data-crystals
			* View as full immersion experiences on the GnuCoder 5000 or in holographic, 2D form on the GnuCoder 3000 here.
			* Data crystals: Letters Home, Do Your Part!, Tibe-Riv’s Primer of Primitive Cultures, the Faithful Manager, Proceedings Against Triv-Lok, Duty Awards, Stardate 6532, How to Talk with the Natives, Our New Home!, Personal Diary of Mol-Prev, Military Instructional Manual, Our Friends, the Kaliyani!, and Voyages of the Shining Beacon of Glorious Heaven (books).
	* Closet:
		* 4 orange jumpsuits (sized for 7’-tall beings), a formal uniform (two piece, orange and blue, with a variety of mission stripes on the sleeves)
			* In the pocket of the dress uniform is a note (Glyphis): “Mol-Prev, Our GnuCoder 5000 has ceased operation. Can you fix it? Since ours is on the fritz, I believe that the machine in the Captain’s Library, near the Cloister, is the only remaining location that can handle our viewing crystals. As it’s quite inconvenient to travel there all the time, I hope you will consider a brief trip to the alchemical pits in order to repair my team’s GnuCoder. It would be a shame, both for morale and for intelligence purposes, if all of our data crystals were to remain unwatchable. (signed) Psalor-Ki.”
				* GM Notes: a hint to the use of data-crystals, the location of an operable GnuCoder 5000 (the library, 5-97), points to the domain of Psalor-Ki, once alchemical chief, now a deranged vivisectionist (5-66 to 5-75).
		* A leather pouch (brown, sky blue, and platinum identity plaques.
		* A rubberized party mask of a grinning varumani.

### 6-118: Residential Pod of the Beacon, Lower Level

* For many centuries, the entire lower level of the Residential Pod has been the lair of a horrendous sumuksu, a spawn of Rimmaq-Isfet (new).
	* Deriving energy from the nuclear generator in 6-123, where its primary protoplasm resides, it has poured its slime through the LED strips into every corner of the level.
		* Most surfaces are slimy and viscous.
		* The greater slime generated subsidiary slimes, dripping from the overhead lighting stripes, that animate living or dead creatures.
	* A small army of animated slime-zombies will attempt to overwhelm intruders and add their bodies to the greater slime’s forces.
	* The greater slime has not been able to re-navigate the null-grav shaft, and is confined to the lower level of the residential pod.
* The central, oval area (6-118) of curved white plasteel has two eye-shaped ovals of grey plasteel marking the null-grav shafts.
	* One ascends to the upper level by entering a fields, kicking off, and arrives at 6-113.
	* The entire area reeks of acid, decay, and corroded plastics.
	* A 3’-wide smear of corroded brown plasteel leads from the western null-grav shaft north towards 6-120, then west into 6-121.
	* A score of smaller corrosive ‘burns’ mar the floor, and another score the wall; all the product of the slime creature.
	* Three 3’-diameter pools of quiescent purple slime dot the floor between the corpses of eight beings.
	* The LED strip lighting that runs through the center of the chamber (and hallways) is no longer a peaceful yellow, but a glistening, sickly purple, from which numerous drips seem about to fall.

* 1d4 rounds after any enter the lower level, 8 slime zombies lumber to their feet/paws and attack.  They are joined by fellows from 6-119 and 6-120 within 1d6 rounds.
* 2d4 heqeti slimes (of the flesh-animating sort) cling to the lighting strips, ready to drop on any plausible host (adventurer or a recently-slain slime zombie).

8 heqeti slime zombies (see new monsters): SZ S(x3), M(x3) and L(x2); AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 2(x3), 4(x3), 6(x2); HP 42, 39, 29, 27, 14, 10; #AT 1; Dmg 2-8. Special attacks: slime infestation. Special defenses: immune to electricity.

2d4 heqeti slimes (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 5’ (creeping); HD 2; HP 14, 13, 13, 12, 12, 11, 11, 10; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: flesh animating (covers flesh and kills victim in 4-7 rounds, then re-animates as a heqeti slime zombie - see new monsters); corrosive to metal, leather, and wood. Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.
* These slimes vary in color and texture, although all are flesh animating; roll for types in new monster appendix.

### 6-119: Slime Covered Lounge

* This lounge contains a number of orange plastic chairs, settees and sofas arranged in clumps around small tables.
	* The north wall is a viewscreen, attuned to display the cavern outside (6-112).
	* The LED lighting strips are fewer, only along the east and west walls, for gentler light.
		* The strips drip slime like those in 6-118.
	* All furniture is covered with a thin layer of sticky slime.
	* Six slime zombies are draped about the room
		* They are likely encountered in 6-118, joining any combat there in 1-6 rounds.
 
6 heqeti slime zombies (see new monsters): SZ S(x2), M(x2) and L(x2); AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 2(x2), 4(x2), 6(x2); HP 42, 39, 29, 27, 14, 10; #AT 1; Dmg 2-8. Special attacks: slime infestation. Special defenses: immune to electricity.

2-8 heqeti slimes (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 5’ (creeping); HD 2; HP 14, 13, 13, 12, 12, 11, 11, 10; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: flesh animating (covers flesh and kills victim in 4-7 rounds, then re-animates as a heqeti slime zombie - see new monsters); corrosive to metal, leather, and wood. Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.
* These slimes vary in color and texture, although all are flesh animating.  Roll for types in new monster appendix.

### 6-120: Slime Covered Refectory

* This area used to be the refectory for the inhabitants of this pod.
	* In its center is a 4’ tall, oval counter with 16 food stations (see 5-109).
		* Each has a silver oval inset and curved yellow tube extending from the counter  over the plate. A row of six colored buttons occupies the front of each station.
		* Pressing buttons spurts various varieties of high-protein, high-vitamin, food paste from the nozzle (not very appetizing, but highly nutritious).
	* A dozen stools set into the floor line the east and west walls.
	* The north wall is a huge viewscreen displaying a live view of 5-94 (the Cloister).
	* The whole area is covered with a layer of sticky slime, and the lighting strips also drip slime.
* Six heqeti slime zombies occupy the room, though they will be drawn into combat at 6-118 in 1d6 rounds.

6 heqeti slime zombies (see new monsters): SZ S(x2), M(x2) and L(x2); AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 2(x2), 4(x2), 6(x2); HP 42, 39, 29, 27, 14, 10; #AT 1; Dmg 2-8. Special attacks: slime infestation. Special defenses: immune to electricity.
* One rudishva slime zombie (6 HD) has a harness holding a sonic fence (fully charged lesser power supply) and a 1’-square jade box (250 gp) holding a sky blue identity plaque.

2-8 heqeti slimes (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 5’ (creeping); HD 2; HP 14, 13, 13, 12, 12, 11, 11, 10; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: flesh animating (covers flesh and kills victim in 4-7 rounds, then re-animates as a heqeti slime zombie - see new monsters); corrosive to metal, leather, and wood. Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold. These slimes vary in color and texture, although all are flesh animating; roll for types in new monster appendix.

### 6-121: Slime Central! (aka Game Room) 

* This former game room has been the home of a sumuksu for close to three millennia, ever since it helped the heqeti breach the residence pod and overwhelm the crewmembers still living here.
	* Both iris doors have been eaten open by the slime, leaving 5’-diameter holes as access points.
	* About a dozen lumps of mostly shapeless plasteel dot the chamber; former entertainment consoles corroded over the years by the slime creature.
		* A claw machine still works, once the slime covering it has been scraped away.
			* A rectangular table with clear plasteel top and a pair of joysticks.
				* AC 2, 50 hp.  If broken, it discharges electricity for 3d6 w/in 15'.
			* Putting in a token (a gold solidus works ideally) in the slot gives a try (5d6 under DEX) to claim a prize.  Three prizes remain:
				* Powder in a plastic sack; rehydrated, it acts as a potion of clairvoyance, with trippy hallucinatory side-effects.
				* A repli-cube (tech)
				* A communications bracelet (tech)
		* Lodged under a destroyed game table is an adventurer’s backpack.
			* Bag of holding (1,000 lb capacity): 10,000 ancient silver pennies, 1,250 ancient gold solidi, 320 ancient octagonal platinum coins; 6 scrolls  (monster summoning II, polymorph other, cloudkill, wall of force, anti-magic shell, spiritwrack).
		* A magic long sword (+4 defender) lies against the south wall.
	* Four slime zombies are scattered throughout the area, and four random heqeti slimes are moving along the ceiling.
	* A15’-diameter mound of mottled green-and-brown slime sits half in and half out the door to 6-123. The sumuksu!
		* Tracks of purple and brown slime run along the overhead lighting strips to the slime creature.
		* It will have been alerted by combat in 6-118, 6-119 or 6-120.

1 sumuksu (see new monsters): SZ L; AL CE; AC 3; MV 30’; HD 10; HP 71; #AT 4; Dmg 2-8/2-8/2-8/2-8; MR 15%. Special attacks: engulf; create new slimes. Special defenses: corrode metal, wood, leather; half damage from cold and fire; immune to charm, hold, and all mind-based spells.

1 burnt-orange, oily and thick heqeti slime (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 5’ on carbon-based substances; HD 2; HP 13; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6; MR 15%. Special attacks: flesh-eating for 4-7 rounds; corrosive to metal, leather, and wood. Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.

1 rust colored, gluey heqeti slime (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 10’ creeping; HD 2; HP 14; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: hallucinations for 7-12 hours; corrosive to leather. Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.

1 sickly green, melted butter-like heqeti slime (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 15’ (pseudopods); HD 2; HP 12; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: spore-throwing 
(death in 3-18 days unless save at -1). Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.

1 pale lavender, watery heqeti slime (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 0’; HD 2; HP 12; #AT 1; Dmg special; MR 15%. Special attacks: exploding (6-36 in 30’ radius). Special defenses: healed by electricity or lasers; slowed by cold.

### 6-122: Exercise Room and Last Stand

* This exercise room was the site of the last stand of the rudishva crewmen surprised by the assault of the heqeti and the sumuksu.
	* The north lobe of the chamber has a set of rubberized mats and free weights.  The southern lobe has eight treadmills built into the floor, facing a now-inoperable view-screen on the southeast wall.
	* These areas drip with slime, and there are 4 slime zombies – 2 heqeti hoppers, 2 rudishva – in each lobe of the chamber.
		* They are barred from entering the hallway by 6-124 (see below). 
	* Both entrances to the 20’x10’ hallway in front of the door to 6-124 are clouded by a slight yellowish vapor, as if from a light mist.
		* The mist is harmless and provide a safe zone from heqeti slimes.
		* The vapor emanates from a thick, yellowish paste painted in a continuous band along the walls, floor and ceiling of each entrance to this corridor.
		* In the corridor lie the desiccated corpses of 8 rudishva and 1 kaliyani.
			* A plasteel bucket of quietly burbling yellow paste rests by their side; enough to cover a medium sized person or to paint a 6” x 40' stripe.
			* Bodies: laser rifle; 2 laser pistols; sonic fence; identity plaques (rust, brown, orange); a repli-cube; 3 lesser power supplies (1, 3, and 2 charges).

GM Notes
* The yellow paste (av items) is a biological, anti-slime agent developed secretly by the kaliyani after they began to plan the ‘great betrayal’ to protect themselves from their new ‘allies’, the heqeti and their slimes.
	* One kaliyani who remained loyal to the rudishva, Kesstak, stole a pot of this anti-slime material and hastened to the residential pod after the attack began.
	* Kesstak and the remaining rudishva painted the substance on the walls of the corridor, saving themselves from the slime creature.
	* Sadly, Captain Leil-Jor shut down the teleporter in 6-124 to avoid contamination, and Kesstak and the other rudishva gradually expired of thirst.
* If activated the repli-cube shows:
	* 1) A desperate battle between orange jumpsuited rudishva and various freshly-made rudishva slime zombies.
	* 2) Arrival of a kaliyani from the door (to 6-124) and excited discussion about the contents of the pail.
	* 3) They frantically painting the walls with yellow paste from the pail.
	* 4) A testimonial from a single rudishva, going in detail about the extraordinary loyalty and heroism of Kesstak, ‘regardless of what his egg-mates may have done elsewhere.’
	* This repli-cube might be worth up to 1,000 gp to the kaliyani leader, Tsilliv (SL9-77), if one can get her to negotiate.

North lobe: 4 heqeti slime zombies (see new monsters): SZ M(x2) and L(x2); AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 4(x2), 6(x2); HP 42, 39, 29, 27; #AT 1; Dmg 2-8. Special attacks: slime infestation. Special defenses: immune to electricity.

South lobe: 4 heqeti slime zombies (see new monsters): SZ M(x2) and L(x2); AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 4(x2), 6(x2); HP 42, 39, 29, 27; #AT 1; Dmg 2-8. Special attacks: slime infestation. Special defenses: immune to electricity.

### 6-123: Generator

* A powerful nuclear-powered generator occupies most of this small closet; providing power to the residential pod since the rudishva days.
	* A bank of plasteel dotted with dials, LED screens, and one keyboard.
	* Difficult to damage short of high-level magic.  If breached, 20d6 explosion to all inside the pod or 6-112, destroying the lower level of the pod.
* The sumuksu has been feeding off its energy for millennia.

### 6-124: Transport Closet

* The iris door to this closet opens to a sky blue, pale green, pink, orange, silver or yellow rudishva identity plaque.
* Originally a supply closet, it was refitted after the crash with a teleport node.
	* T3: access to 5-92 (transport hall)
	* GM Note: this node was disabled during the last days of the rudishva in Arden Vul, but restored by Psalor-Ki years later.

### 6-125: Warm Cavern

* Unlike areas further west (6-136 to 6-142), this cave is warm and humid.
	* A number of moderate sized mushrooms grow here (4’ to 8’).
	* Hidden behind the mushrooms is a ledge 15’ up the south wall, with a tunnel leading south.

### 6-126: Dead Lizards

* This rocky cave rises slightly towards the south.
	* The slight elevation change changes climate, from cold, dry northern tunnels (to 6-139) to the warm, humid southern portion.
	* Three 15’-long subterranean lizard corpses sprawl before the eastern tunnel.
		* Marks of intense searing (laser fire); killed by the adventurers in 6-113.

### 6-127: Corpsicles

* Two frozen adventurers lie amid the stalagmites and stalactites, slowly melting.
	* They were slain in 6-140 and dragged here by their friends, who left to seek assistance but never returned.
	* The encasing ice will melt away in 1d6+3 hours.
	* Warrior: 69 cp, 58 sp, 35 gp; long sword; scale mail; potion of heroism
	* Mage: staff; ring of protection +1.

### 6-128: Chasm Access

* This unoccupied cave is sandy and relatively flat.  It provides clear and easy access to the Great Chasm (6-108).
	* A handful of jumbled skeletons (several humans, a grimalkin, a heqeti and a varumani) rest against the southwest wall (no valuables or gear).
	* Obvious boot prints lead south.
* Spending more than 3 turns here has a 50% chance to attract an encounter from the Great Chasm (middle levels table – see 6-108).
	* Campers here will be visited by a pod of chasm cephalopods.

### 6-129: Base Camp

* The Bad Neighbors adventuring party has established its base camp in this humid but sandy cave.
	* Most of them currently explore 6-113, while 3 junior members guard the supplies.
		* Cyricus is sitting on a small metal chest.
			* Metal chest (locked, poison needle): sapphire Sortian eye; 6 deep blue spinels (500 gp each); 6 octagonal platinum coins; 2 doses of hunter’s friend (av items); a platinum decanter (475 gp).
	* Four bearers crouch nervously around the fire.
	* Four sacks of food and supplies, plus a barrel of fresh water, line the cave wall behind a small wood-fire fire.
		* Sack #1: dried food rations for 10 people for a week.
		* Sack #2: trade goods: 250 colored glass beads (25 sp total), 25 skeins of colored yarn (3 gp each), 12 bottles of red wine (25 gp each), 4 quivers with 12 crossbow bolts in each (25 sp each), and 20 sugary delicacies (5 sp each).
		* Sack #3: 10 10-lb silver ingots (25 gp each).
		* Sack #4: adventuring equipment
